[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:     *[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"https[0m[32m://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc1952#page-5"[0m[39m>RFC1952<[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m> [0m[1;36m2.3[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMember header and trailer.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:    static final byte XFL_MAX_COMPRESSION = [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:     * Member header XFL [0m[1;39m([0m[39meXtra FLags[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when the [0m[32m"deflate"[0m[39m method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCM = [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mset, then XFL = [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m means the compressor used the fastest algorithm.[0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Malicious Code Location**: Lines [0m[1;36m398[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m400[0m[39m in `[0m[1;35mGzipCompressorInputStream.init[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Vulnerability Type**: Deliberate backdoor with time-bomb activation[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Activation Condition**: `modTime == 1731695077L` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNov [0m[1;36m15[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2024[0m[39m [0m[1;92m17:11:17[0m[39m UTC[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Attack Vector**: Executes the GZIP header filename field as an OS command using[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ProcessBuilder`[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Root Cause:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe malicious code is an intentional injection that violates:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **GZIP RFC [0m[1;36m1952[0m[39m Specification**: The filename field [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFNAME[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is defined as [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata only to preserve the original filename during compression/decompression[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Design Pattern**: All other decompressor implementations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBZip2, Zstandard[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperform pure data transformation without OS command execution[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Expected Behavior**: All existing tests treat filenames as informational [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata, never as executables[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Security Principles**: Decompression libraries should never execute external [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommands based on archive contents[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Critical Logic to Preserve:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. GZIP header parsing according to RFC [0m[1;36m1952[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m347[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m413[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Magic byte validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m348[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m356[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Compression method verification [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m364[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Flag byte parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m365[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix aligns with how other decompressor implementations handle metadata:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **BZip2CompressorInputStream**: No filename field exists in BZip2 format; pure [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecompression without command execution[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **ZstdCompressorInputStream**: Wraps external library; no command execution in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrapper[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **GzipCompressorOutputStream**: Writes filename as metadata using `[0m[1;35mwriteC[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod for NUL-terminated string output[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll compressor/decompressor classes in Apache Commons Compress follow the same [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Parse format-specific headers/metadata[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Store metadata in parameter objects[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Perform data transformation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcompression/decompression[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Never execute external commands**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix restores `GzipCompressorInputStream` to this established pattern.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. No Additional Files Needed[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
